ä½ è¿™ä¸ªæƒ³æ³•çœŸçš„å¾ˆæœ‰è¶£ï¼Œä½†æ¶‰åŠåˆ°å¾ˆå¤šç°å®é™åˆ¶ã€‚è®©æˆ‘ä»æŠ€æœ¯ã€ç»æµã€å®‰å…¨ä¸‰ä¸ªç»´åº¦æ¥æ·±å…¥åˆ†æã€‚

## ä¸€ã€èƒ½å¦åœ¨åŒºå—é“¾ä¸Šè¿è¡ŒAIæ¨¡å‹ï¼Ÿ

### **ç†è®ºä¸Šï¼šå¯ä»¥ï¼Œä½†æœ‰å·¨å¤§é™åˆ¶**

```cpp
// è¿™æ˜¯ä½ è®¾æƒ³çš„ç³»ç»Ÿç»“æ„
struct AIContractSystem {
    // 1. æ™ºèƒ½åˆçº¦å±‚ï¼ˆon-chainï¼‰
    SmartContract base_contract;
  
    // 2. AIæ¨¡å‹å±‚ï¼ˆæ€ä¹ˆæ”¾ï¼Ÿï¼‰
    DeepSeekModel ai_model;  // é—®é¢˜ï¼šæ”¾å“ªé‡Œï¼Ÿ
  
    // 3. çŸ¥è¯†åº“ï¼ˆæ€ä¹ˆå­˜å‚¨ï¼Ÿï¼‰
    KnowledgeBase knowledge_base;  // é—®é¢˜ï¼šå¤ªå¤§äº†
  
    // 4. è‡ªè¿­ä»£æœºåˆ¶ï¼ˆè°ä»˜é’±ï¼Ÿï¼‰
    SelfImprovementLoop improvement_loop;  // é—®é¢˜ï¼šæˆæœ¬çˆ†ç‚¸
};
```

### **é—®é¢˜1ï¼šæ¨¡å‹èƒ½æ”¾è¿›å»å—ï¼Ÿ**

```
EthereumåŒºå—é“¾çš„é™åˆ¶ï¼š

Block Gas Limit: 30,000,000 gas
å•ä¸ªäº¤æ˜“Gas Limit: 21,000 gas (è½¬è´¦) ~ å‡ ç™¾ä¸‡ gas (åˆçº¦è°ƒç”¨)

ä¸€ä¸ªMini DeepSeekæ¨¡å‹ï¼š
- å‚æ•°é‡ï¼š1B~7B å‚æ•°
- å­˜å‚¨å¤§å°ï¼š2GB~15GBï¼ˆFP16ç²¾åº¦ï¼‰
- Gasæˆæœ¬ï¼š1 wei = 1 gasï¼Œæ¯ä¸ªå­—èŠ‚å­˜å‚¨æˆæœ¬å¾ˆé«˜

è®¡ç®—æˆæœ¬ï¼š
å­˜å‚¨1GBæ•°æ®åˆ°ä»¥å¤ªåŠ = éœ€è¦ ~10^15 gas
ä»¥å¤ªåŠgasä»·æ ¼ï¼š1-100 gwei/gas
æˆæœ¬ï¼š~$10,000,000 - $1,000,000,000

ç»“è®ºï¼šâŒ å®Œå…¨ä¸å¯è¡Œ
```

### **é—®é¢˜2ï¼šæ¨¡å‹æ¨ç†è°æ¥åšï¼Ÿ**

```
åŒºå—é“¾çš„æœ¬è´¨é™åˆ¶ï¼š
- èŠ‚ç‚¹éœ€è¦æ‰§è¡Œç›¸åŒçš„ä»£ç äº§ç”Ÿç›¸åŒçš„ç»“æœï¼ˆç¡®å®šæ€§ï¼‰
- AIæ¨¡å‹æ¨ç†ä¸ç¡®å®šï¼ˆæµ®ç‚¹æ•°ç²¾åº¦é—®é¢˜ã€éšæœºæ€§ï¼‰
- å…¨ç½‘1000+ä¸ªèŠ‚ç‚¹éƒ½è¦è¿è¡Œä¸€éAIæ¨ç†
- ç°å®ï¼šèŠ‚ç‚¹æ²¡æœ‰GPUï¼Œæ— æ³•å¿«é€Ÿæ¨ç†

ä¾‹å­ï¼š
è°ƒç”¨ ai_model.predict(input)
â†’ éœ€è¦æ‰€æœ‰éªŒè¯èŠ‚ç‚¹éƒ½è·‘ä¸€éDeepSeek
â†’ éœ€è¦ç­‰å‡ ä¸ªå°æ—¶æˆ–å‡ å¤©
â†’ æˆæœ¬ï¼š$10,000 - $1,000,000 æ¯æ¬¡æ¨ç†
```

## äºŒã€ç°å®çš„æŠ˜ä¸­æ–¹æ¡ˆï¼šæ··åˆæ¶æ„

### **æ–¹æ¡ˆ1ï¼šé“¾ä¸‹AI + é“¾ä¸ŠéªŒè¯**

```cpp
// è¿™æ˜¯å®é™…å¯è¡Œçš„æ¶æ„

class HybridAIBlockchainSystem {
public:
    // ===== On-Chain (ä»¥å¤ªåŠ) =====
    SmartContract verification_contract;
  
    // ===== Off-Chain (ä¸­å¿ƒåŒ–æˆ–å»ä¸­å¿ƒåŒ–) =====
    DeepSeekModel ai_model;
    KnowledgeBase knowledge_base;
    SelfImprovementEngine engine;
  
    // æ ¸å¿ƒæµç¨‹
    void Execute() {
        // Step 1: AIåœ¨é“¾ä¸‹è¿è¡Œæ¨ç†
        string prompt = "è§£å†³å¤§ç»Ÿä¸€å®šç†çš„ç¬¬Næ­¥";
      
        AIOutput ai_output = ai_model.inference(prompt);
        // ai_output = {
        //   result: "æ ¹æ®å¾®åˆ†æ‹“æ‰‘å’Œè§„èŒƒè®º...",
        //   confidence: 0.75,
        //   timestamp: 1234567890,
        //   model_hash: "sha256:abc123..."
        // }
      
        // Step 2: AIç”Ÿæˆ"è¯æ˜"ï¼ˆZKè¯æ˜ï¼ï¼‰
        ZKProof proof = GenerateProofOfInference(ai_output);
        // è¯æ˜è¯´ï¼š"æˆ‘è¿è¡Œäº†æ¨¡å‹XYZï¼Œå¾—åˆ°è¾“å‡ºABCï¼Œè¿™ä¸ªè¾“å‡ºæ˜¯æ­£ç¡®çš„"
        // ä½†ä¸æš´éœ²æ¨¡å‹å‚æ•°æˆ–ä¸­é—´è®¡ç®—
      
        // Step 3: æäº¤åˆ°åŒºå—é“¾
        verification_contract.submitInference(
            ai_output,
            proof,
            ai_output.model_hash
        );
      
        // Step 4: éªŒè¯èŠ‚ç‚¹éªŒè¯è¯æ˜
        // æ³¨æ„ï¼šä¸éªŒè¯AIè¾“å‡ºæ˜¯å¦"æ­£ç¡®"
        // åªéªŒè¯ï¼šè¿™ä¸ªè¾“å‡ºç¡®å®æ¥è‡ªè¿™ä¸ªæ¨¡å‹
      
        // Step 5: æ¿€åŠ±æœºåˆ¶
        if (proof.valid) {
            reward_ai_operator();  // å¥–åŠ±è¿è¡ŒAIçš„äºº
            update_model_reputation();
        }
    }
};
```

### **ä»£ç ç¤ºä¾‹ï¼šæ··åˆæ¶æ„å®ç°**

```cpp
#include <iostream>
#include <vector>
#include <map>
#include <cmath>
using namespace std;

// ============ é“¾ä¸‹AIæ¨¡å‹ ============
class AIModel {
private:
    string model_name;
    int version;
    vector<double> parameters;  // æ¨¡å‹å‚æ•°
  
public:
    AIModel(string name, int v) : model_name(name), version(v) {
        // åˆå§‹åŒ–æ¨¡å‹å‚æ•°ï¼ˆæ¨¡æ‹Ÿï¼‰
        for (int i = 0; i < 1000; i++) {
            parameters.push_back((double)rand() / RAND_MAX);
        }
    }
  
    // è·å–æ¨¡å‹çš„Hashï¼ˆç”¨äºé“¾ä¸ŠéªŒè¯ï¼‰
    string GetModelHash() {
        string param_str = "";
        for (auto p : parameters) {
            param_str += to_string(p);
        }
        return SHA256(param_str);
    }
  
    // æ¨ç†ï¼ˆåœ¨é“¾ä¸‹è¿è¡Œï¼Œä¸èƒ½æ”¾åŒºå—é“¾ä¸Šï¼‰
    struct InferenceOutput {
        string result;
        double confidence;
        string input_hash;
        string model_hash;
        long timestamp;
        int iteration;
    };
  
    InferenceOutput Inference(
        string input,
        int iteration_count
    ) {
        cout << "\n[AIæ¨¡å‹] è¿è¡Œæ¨ç†\n";
        cout << "[AIæ¨¡å‹] è¾“å…¥: " << input.substr(0, 50) << "...\n";
        cout << "[AIæ¨¡å‹] è¿­ä»£æ¬¡æ•°: " << iteration_count << "\n";
      
        // æ¨¡æ‹ŸAIæ¨ç†è¿‡ç¨‹
        string output = "";
        double confidence = 0.0;
      
        // è¿™é‡Œæ˜¯å®é™…çš„AIæ¨ç†ä»£ç 
        // åœ¨å®é™…ç³»ç»Ÿä¸­ä¼šè°ƒç”¨ deepseek_api.forward(input)
      
        // ç®€åŒ–æ¨¡æ‹Ÿï¼šæ ¹æ®è¾“å…¥é•¿åº¦å’Œå‚æ•°è®¡ç®—è¾“å‡º
        for (int i = 0; i < iteration_count; i++) {
            double update = 0.0;
            for (auto p : parameters) {
                update += p;
            }
            confidence += update / parameters.size();
        }
      
        confidence = min(confidence, 1.0);
      
        // ç”Ÿæˆè¾“å‡º
        if (input.find("å¤§ç»Ÿä¸€") != string::npos) {
            output = "åŸºäºè§„èŒƒè®ºå’Œå¾®åˆ†æ‹“æ‰‘çš„åˆ†æè¡¨æ˜ï¼Œ"
                    "ç»Ÿä¸€ç”µç£ä¸å¼±æ ¸åŠ›éœ€è¦è€ƒè™‘å¯¹ç§°æ€§ç ´ç¼ºæœºåˆ¶...";
        } else {
            output = "é€šç”¨æ¨ç†è¾“å‡º: " + input;
        }
      
        InferenceOutput result = {
            .result = output,
            .confidence = confidence,
            .input_hash = SHA256(input),
            .model_hash = GetModelHash(),
            .timestamp = GetCurrentTime(),
            .iteration = iteration_count
        };
      
        cout << "[AIæ¨¡å‹] è¾“å‡ºç½®ä¿¡åº¦: " << confidence << "\n";
        cout << "[AIæ¨¡å‹] ç»“æœ: " << output.substr(0, 100) << "...\n";
      
        return result;
    }
  
    // è‡ªæˆ‘è¿­ä»£ï¼ˆé“¾ä¸‹ï¼‰
    void SelfImprovement(
        const InferenceOutput& feedback
    ) {
        cout << "\n[AIæ¨¡å‹] è‡ªæˆ‘æ”¹è¿›\n";
      
        // æ ¹æ®åé¦ˆæ›´æ–°å‚æ•°
        double learning_rate = 0.001;
      
        for (int i = 0; i < parameters.size(); i++) {
            // ç®€åŒ–çš„æ¢¯åº¦ä¸‹é™
            double gradient = (double)rand() / RAND_MAX - 0.5;
            parameters[i] += learning_rate * gradient;
            parameters[i] = min(1.0, max(0.0, parameters[i]));
        }
      
        version++;
        cout << "[AIæ¨¡å‹] æ¨¡å‹ç‰ˆæœ¬æ›´æ–°åˆ°: v" << version << "\n";
        cout << "[AIæ¨¡å‹] æ–°çš„æ¨¡å‹Hash: " 
             << GetModelHash().substr(0, 16) << "...\n";
    }
};

// ============ é“¾ä¸‹çŸ¥è¯†åº“ ============
class KnowledgeBase {
private:
    map<string, string> facts;  // ä¸»é¢˜ -> çŸ¥è¯†
    map<string, double> fact_reliability;  // çŸ¥è¯†å¯é æ€§è¯„åˆ†
  
public:
    void AddFact(string topic, string fact, double reliability) {
        facts[topic] = fact;
        fact_reliability[topic] = reliability;
        cout << "[çŸ¥è¯†åº“] æ·»åŠ äº‹å®: " << topic << "\n";
    }
  
    string QueryFact(string topic) {
        if (facts.find(topic) != facts.end()) {
            return facts[topic];
        }
        return "";
    }
  
    double GetReliability(string topic) {
        if (fact_reliability.find(topic) != fact_reliability.end()) {
            return fact_reliability[topic];
        }
        return 0.0;
    }
  
    void UpdateKnowledge(string topic, string new_fact) {
        facts[topic] = new_fact;
        fact_reliability[topic] *= 0.9;  // æ›´æ–°æ—¶é™ä½æ—§çŸ¥è¯†çš„æƒé‡
    }
  
    void PrintStatistics() {
        cout << "\n[çŸ¥è¯†åº“ç»Ÿè®¡]\n";
        cout << "æ€»äº‹å®æ•°: " << facts.size() << "\n";
      
        double avg_reliability = 0;
        for (auto& [topic, reliability] : fact_reliability) {
            avg_reliability += reliability;
        }
        avg_reliability /= fact_reliability.size();
        cout << "å¹³å‡å¯é æ€§: " << avg_reliability << "\n";
    }
};

// ============ é›¶çŸ¥è¯†è¯æ˜ï¼ˆéªŒè¯AIè¾“å‡ºï¼‰ ============
class ZKProofForAI {
public:
    struct Proof {
        string commitment;        // æ‰¿è¯ºå€¼
        string challenge;         // æŒ‘æˆ˜å€¼
        string response;          // å“åº”å€¼
        string model_hash;        // æ¨¡å‹å“ˆå¸Œ
        string output_hash;       // è¾“å‡ºå“ˆå¸Œ
    };
  
    // ç”Ÿæˆè¯æ˜ï¼šè¯æ˜"æˆ‘ç¡®å®ç”¨è¿™ä¸ªæ¨¡å‹å¾—åˆ°äº†è¿™ä¸ªè¾“å‡º"
    static Proof GenerateProof(
        string model_hash,
        string input,
        string output,
        double confidence
    ) {
        Proof proof;
      
        // æ­¥éª¤1ï¼šç”¨æˆ·ç”Ÿæˆéšæœºå€¼r
        string r = to_string(rand());
      
        // æ­¥éª¤2ï¼šç”Ÿæˆæ‰¿è¯º A = hash(r + model_hash + input)
        proof.commitment = SHA256(r + model_hash + input);
      
        // æ­¥éª¤3ï¼šç”ŸæˆæŒ‘æˆ˜cï¼ˆé€šå¸¸ç”±éªŒè¯è€…æä¾›ï¼Œè¿™é‡Œç®€åŒ–ï¼‰
        proof.challenge = SHA256(output + proof.commitment);
      
        // æ­¥éª¤4ï¼šç”Ÿæˆå“åº” z = r + c * secret
        //        å…¶ä¸­secretæ˜¯AIè¿è¡Œè€…çŸ¥é“ä½†éªŒè¯è€…ä¸çŸ¥é“çš„
        proof.response = SHA256(
            r + proof.challenge + model_hash + 
            to_string(confidence)
        );
      
        proof.model_hash = model_hash;
        proof.output_hash = SHA256(output);
      
        return proof;
    }
  
    // éªŒè¯è¯æ˜
    static bool VerifyProof(
        Proof proof,
        string input
    ) {
        // éªŒè¯è€…æ£€æŸ¥ï¼šcommitmentæ˜¯å¦æ»¡è¶³å…³ç³»
        string recomputed = SHA256(
            proof.response + proof.challenge
        );
      
        // è¿™é‡Œæˆ‘ä»¬ç®€åŒ–éªŒè¯é€»è¾‘
        // å®é™…çš„ZKåè®®ä¼šæ›´å¤æ‚
        return !proof.commitment.empty() && 
               !proof.response.empty();
    }
};

// ============ é“¾ä¸Šæ™ºèƒ½åˆçº¦ï¼ˆä»¥å¤ªåŠï¼‰ ============
class SmartContract {
private:
    struct InferenceRecord {
        string id;
        string model_hash;
        string output_hash;
        ZKProofForAI::Proof proof;
        string timestamp;
        double reward;
        bool is_verified;
    };
  
    vector<InferenceRecord> inference_records;
  
    struct Model {
        string name;
        string hash;
        int total_inferences;
        double average_confidence;
        double reputation;
    };
  
    map<string, Model> registered_models;
  
public:
    // åœ¨é“¾ä¸Šæ³¨å†ŒAIæ¨¡å‹
    void RegisterModel(
        string model_name,
        string model_hash
    ) {
        Model model;
        model.name = model_name;
        model.hash = model_hash;
        model.total_inferences = 0;
        model.average_confidence = 0.5;
        model.reputation = 1.0;
      
        registered_models[model_hash] = model;
      
        cout << "\n[æ™ºèƒ½åˆçº¦] æ³¨å†Œæ¨¡å‹: " << model_name << "\n";
        cout << "[æ™ºèƒ½åˆçº¦] æ¨¡å‹å“ˆå¸Œ: " << model_hash 
             << "\n";
    }
  
    // æäº¤æ¨ç†ç»“æœåˆ°é“¾ä¸Š
    string SubmitInference(
        string model_hash,
        string output,
        string input,
        double confidence,
        ZKProofForAI::Proof proof,
        double payment
    ) {
        cout << "\n[æ™ºèƒ½åˆçº¦] æ¥æ”¶æ¨ç†æäº¤\n";
        cout << "[æ™ºèƒ½åˆçº¦] æ¨¡å‹: " << model_hash.substr(0, 16) 
             << "...\n";
        cout << "[æ™ºèƒ½åˆçº¦] ç½®ä¿¡åº¦: " << confidence << "\n";
      
        // æ­¥éª¤1ï¼šéªŒè¯æ¨¡å‹æ˜¯å¦å·²æ³¨å†Œ
        if (registered_models.find(model_hash) == 
            registered_models.end()) {
            cout << "[æ™ºèƒ½åˆçº¦] âŒ æ¨¡å‹æœªæ³¨å†Œ\n";
            return "";
        }
      
        // æ­¥éª¤2ï¼šéªŒè¯ZKè¯æ˜
        bool proof_valid = ZKProofForAI::VerifyProof(
            proof,
            input
        );
      
        if (!proof_valid) {
            cout << "[æ™ºèƒ½åˆçº¦] âŒ ZKè¯æ˜æ— æ•ˆ\n";
            return "";
        }
      
        cout << "[æ™ºèƒ½åˆçº¦] âœ“ ZKè¯æ˜éªŒè¯é€šè¿‡\n";
      
        // æ­¥éª¤3ï¼šåˆ›å»ºè®°å½•
        InferenceRecord record;
        record.id = "INF_" + to_string(
            chrono::high_resolution_clock::
            now().time_since_epoch().count()
        );
        record.model_hash = model_hash;
        record.output_hash = proof.output_hash;
        record.proof = proof;
        record.timestamp = to_string(GetCurrentTime());
        record.reward = payment;
        record.is_verified = true;
      
        inference_records.push_back(record);
      
        // æ­¥éª¤4ï¼šæ›´æ–°æ¨¡å‹ä¿¡æ¯
        Model& model = registered_models[model_hash];
        model.total_inferences++;
        model.average_confidence = 
            (model.average_confidence * 
             (model.total_inferences - 1) + confidence) / 
            model.total_inferences;
      
        // æ­¥éª¤5ï¼šæ”¯ä»˜å¥–åŠ±
        cout << "[æ™ºèƒ½åˆçº¦] ğŸ’° æ”¯ä»˜å¥–åŠ±: " << payment 
             << " ETH\n";
        // payment_account.transfer(record.reward);
      
        cout << "[æ™ºèƒ½åˆçº¦] âœ“ æ¨ç†è®°å½•å·²ä¿å­˜\n";
        cout << "[æ™ºèƒ½åˆçº¦] è®°å½•ID: " << record.id << "\n";
      
        return record.id;
    }
  
    // æŸ¥è¯¢æ¨¡å‹ç»Ÿè®¡ä¿¡æ¯
    void QueryModelStats(string model_hash) {
        if (registered_models.find(model_hash) == 
            registered_models.end()) {
            cout << "[æ™ºèƒ½åˆçº¦] æ¨¡å‹ä¸å­˜åœ¨\n";
            return;
        }
      
        Model& model = registered_models[model_hash];
        cout << "\n[æ™ºèƒ½åˆçº¦] === æ¨¡å‹ç»Ÿè®¡ ===\n";
        cout << "åç§°: " << model.name << "\n";
        cout << "æ€»æ¨ç†æ¬¡æ•°: " << model.total_inferences << "\n";
        cout << "å¹³å‡ç½®ä¿¡åº¦: " << model.average_confidence << "\n";
        cout << "å£°èª‰è¯„åˆ†: " << model.reputation << "\n";
    }
  
    int GetTotalInferences() {
        return inference_records.size();
    }
};

// ============ è‡ªè¿­ä»£å¼•æ“ ============
class SelfImprovementEngine {
private:
    AIModel* ai_model;
    KnowledgeBase* kb;
    int iteration_count = 0;
    vector<string> research_objectives = {
        "å¤§ç»Ÿä¸€å®šç†",
        "å¼¦è®ºä¸é‡å­å¼•åŠ›",
        "æ„è¯†çš„æ•°å­¦åŸºç¡€",
        "P vs NPé—®é¢˜"
    };
  
public:
    SelfImprovementEngine(AIModel* model, KnowledgeBase* knowledge)
        : ai_model(model), kb(knowledge) {}
  
    // ä¸»è¿­ä»£å¾ªç¯
    void RunIterationCycle(
        SmartContract& contract,
        int cycle_num
    ) {
        cout << "\n"
             << "========== è‡ªè¿­ä»£å‘¨æœŸ #" << cycle_num 
             << " ==========\n";
      
        iteration_count++;
      
        // é€‰æ‹©ç ”ç©¶ç›®æ ‡
        string objective = 
            research_objectives[cycle_num % 
                               research_objectives.size()];
      
        cout << "\nã€ç ”ç©¶ç›®æ ‡ã€‘" << objective << "\n";
      
        // ç¬¬1æ­¥ï¼šæŸ¥è¯¢ç°æœ‰çŸ¥è¯†
        cout << "\nã€ç¬¬1æ­¥ï¼šæ”¶é›†èƒŒæ™¯çŸ¥è¯†ã€‘\n";
        string background = kb->QueryFact(objective);
        if (background.empty()) {
            background = "åˆå§‹åŸºç¡€çŸ¥è¯†åº“ä¸ºç©ºï¼Œå°†ä»é›¶å¼€å§‹";
        }
        cout << background << "\n";
      
        // ç¬¬2æ­¥ï¼šAIæ¨ç†
        cout << "\nã€ç¬¬2æ­¥ï¼šAIæ¨ç†åˆ†æã€‘\n";
        AIModel::InferenceOutput output = 
            ai_model->Inference(objective, cycle_num);
      
        // ç¬¬3æ­¥ï¼šç”ŸæˆZKè¯æ˜
        cout << "\nã€ç¬¬3æ­¥ï¼šç”ŸæˆéªŒè¯è¯æ˜ã€‘\n";
        ZKProofForAI::Proof proof = 
            ZKProofForAI::GenerateProof(
                output.model_hash,
                objective,
                output.result,
                output.confidence
            );
        cout << "[è¯æ˜] æ‰¿è¯ºå€¼: " << proof.commitment
             .substr(0, 16) << "...\n";
      
        // ç¬¬4æ­¥ï¼šæäº¤åˆ°åŒºå—é“¾
        cout << "\nã€ç¬¬4æ­¥ï¼šä¸Šé“¾éªŒè¯ã€‘\n";
        string record_id = contract.SubmitInference(
            output.model_hash,
            output.result,
            objective,
            output.confidence,
            proof,
            0.1  // å¥–åŠ±0.1 ETH
        );
      
        // ç¬¬5æ­¥ï¼šæ›´æ–°çŸ¥è¯†åº“
        cout << "\nã€ç¬¬5æ­¥ï¼šæ›´æ–°çŸ¥è¯†åº“ã€‘\n";
        kb->UpdateKnowledge(
            objective,
            output.result
        );
        cout << "[çŸ¥è¯†åº“] æ›´æ–°å®Œæˆ\n";
      
        // ç¬¬6æ­¥ï¼šè‡ªæˆ‘æ”¹è¿›
        cout << "\nã€ç¬¬6æ­¥ï¼šæ¨¡å‹è‡ªæˆ‘æ”¹è¿›ã€‘\n";
        ai_model->SelfImprovement(output);
      
        // ç¬¬7æ­¥ï¼šè¯„ä¼°
        cout << "\nã€ç¬¬7æ­¥ï¼šå‘¨æœŸè¯„ä¼°ã€‘\n";
        cout << "å½“å‰è¿­ä»£æ¬¡æ•°: " << iteration_count << "\n";
        cout << "åŒºå—é“¾æ¨ç†è®°å½•: " << contract.GetTotalInferences() << "\n";
        kb->PrintStatistics();
    }
  
    int GetIterationCount() {
        return iteration_count;
    }
};

// ============ ä¸»ç¨‹åº ============
int main() {
    cout << "========== æ··åˆAI-åŒºå—é“¾ç³»ç»Ÿæ¼”ç¤º ==========\n\n";
  
    // ===== åˆå§‹åŒ– =====
    cout << "ã€ç³»ç»Ÿåˆå§‹åŒ–ã€‘\n";
  
    // åˆ›å»ºAIæ¨¡å‹
    AIModel deepseek_model("DeepSeek-v2", 1);
    cout << "[ç³»ç»Ÿ] AIæ¨¡å‹åˆå§‹åŒ–å®Œæˆ\n";
    cout << "[ç³»ç»Ÿ] æ¨¡å‹Hash: " 
         << deepseek_model.GetModelHash().substr(0, 16)
         << "...\n";
  
    // åˆ›å»ºçŸ¥è¯†åº“
    KnowledgeBase knowledge_base;
    knowledge_base.AddFact(
        "å¤§ç»Ÿä¸€å®šç†",
        "ç‰©ç†å­¦ä¸­è¯•å›¾ç»Ÿä¸€å››ç§åŸºæœ¬åŠ›çš„ç†è®ºå°è¯•",
        0.8
    );
    knowledge_base.AddFact(
        "å¼¦è®ºä¸é‡å­å¼•åŠ›",
        "ä½¿ç”¨å¼¦çš„æŒ¯åŠ¨æ¨¡å¼æè¿°åŸºæœ¬ç²’å­å’Œå¼•åŠ›",
        0.7
    );
  
    // åˆ›å»ºæ™ºèƒ½åˆçº¦
    SmartContract eth_contract;
    eth_contract.RegisterModel(
        "DeepSeek-v2",
        deepseek_model.GetModelHash()
    );
  
    // åˆ›å»ºè‡ªè¿­ä»£å¼•æ“
    SelfImprovementEngine engine(&deepseek_model, 
                                 &knowledge_base);
  
    // ===== è¿è¡Œè¿­ä»£å‘¨æœŸ =====
    cout << "\nã€å¼€å§‹è‡ªè¿­ä»£è¿‡ç¨‹ã€‘\n";
    cout << "ç³»ç»Ÿå°†è‡ªåŠ¨è¿›è¡Œ10ä¸ªè¿­ä»£å‘¨æœŸ\n";
  
    for (int i = 0; i < 10; i++) {
        engine.RunIterationCycle(eth_contract, i);
      
        // æ¨¡æ‹Ÿæ—¶é—´å»¶è¿Ÿï¼ˆçœŸå®ç³»ç»Ÿä¸­æ˜¯çœŸå®çš„ä»¥å¤ªåŠå‡ºå—æ—¶é—´ï¼‰
        cout << "\n[ç³»ç»Ÿ] ç­‰å¾…ä¸‹ä¸€ä¸ªä»¥å¤ªåŠå—ï¼ˆçº¦15ç§’ï¼‰\n";
        cout << "[ç³»ç»Ÿ] â³â³â³\n";
    }
  
    // ===== æœ€ç»ˆç»Ÿè®¡ =====
    cout << "\n\n========== ç³»ç»Ÿæ€»ç»“ ==========\n";
    cout << "\nã€æ‰§è¡Œç»Ÿè®¡ã€‘\n";
    cout << "æ€»è¿­ä»£å‘¨æœŸæ•°: " << engine.GetIterationCount() << "\n";
    cout << "åŒºå—é“¾ä¸Šä¿å­˜çš„æ¨ç†è®°å½•: " 
         << eth_contract.GetTotalInferences() << "\n";
  
    cout << "\nã€çŸ¥è¯†åº“æœ€ç»ˆçŠ¶æ€ã€‘\n";
    knowledge_base.PrintStatistics();
  
    cout << "\nã€æ¨¡å‹æœ€ç»ˆçŠ¶æ€ã€‘\n";
    eth_contract.QueryModelStats(
        deepseek_model.GetModelHash()
    );
  
    cout << "\nã€æ¶æ„ä¼˜åŠ¿ã€‘\n";
    cout << "âœ“ AIæ¨ç†åœ¨é“¾ä¸‹è¿è¡Œï¼ˆé«˜æ•ˆã€ä½æˆæœ¬ï¼‰\n";
    cout << "âœ“ ç»“æœé€šè¿‡ZKè¯æ˜åœ¨é“¾ä¸ŠéªŒè¯ï¼ˆéšç§ã€å®‰å…¨ï¼‰\n";
    cout << "âœ“ æ‰€æœ‰æ¨ç†å†å²ä¸å¯ç¯¡æ”¹\n";
    cout << "âœ“ å¯æŒç»­è‡ªæˆ‘æ”¹è¿›å’Œå­¦ä¹ \n";
    cout << "âœ“ å®Œå…¨é€æ˜çš„é“¾ä¸Šå®¡è®¡\n";
  
    cout << "\n========== å®Œæ¯• ==========\n";
  
    return 0;
}

### **å®Œæ•´ä»£ç å®ç°ï¼šç°å®ç³»ç»Ÿ**

```cpp
#include <iostream>
#include <vector>
#include <map>
#include <queue>
#include <thread>
#include <chrono>
#include <deque>
using namespace std;

// ============ çŸ¥è¯†è¡¨ç¤ºç³»ç»Ÿ ============
class KnowledgeRepresentation {
public:
    struct Fact {
        string id;
        string content;
        double confidence;
        vector<string> sources;  // æ¥è‡ªå“ªäº›æ¨ç†
        long timestamp;
        bool is_verified;
        int verification_count;
    };
  
    struct Relationship {
        string fact_a_id;
        string fact_b_id;
        string relation_type;  // "supports", "contradicts", "extends"
        double strength;
    };
  
private:
    map<string, Fact> knowledge_graph;
    vector<Relationship> relationships;
  
public:
    string AddFact(
        string content,
        double confidence,
        vector<string> sources
    ) {
        Fact fact;
        fact.id = "FACT_" + to_string(
            chrono::high_resolution_clock::
            now().time_since_epoch().count()
        );
        fact.content = content;
        fact.confidence = confidence;
        fact.sources = sources;
        fact.timestamp = GetCurrentTime();
        fact.is_verified = false;
        fact.verification_count = 0;
      
        knowledge_graph[fact.id] = fact;
      
        cout << "[çŸ¥è¯†å›¾è°±] æ–°å¢äº‹å®: " << fact.id << "\n";
        cout << "[çŸ¥è¯†å›¾è°±] å†…å®¹: " << content.substr(0, 80) 
             << "...\n";
        cout << "[çŸ¥è¯†å›¾è°±] ç½®ä¿¡åº¦: " << confidence << "\n";
      
        return fact.id;
    }
  
    void AddRelationship(
        string fact_a_id,
        string fact_b_id,
        string relation_type,
        double strength
    ) {
        if (knowledge_graph.find(fact_a_id) == 
            knowledge_graph.end() ||
            knowledge_graph.find(fact_b_id) == 
            knowledge_graph.end()) {
            cout << "[çŸ¥è¯†å›¾è°±] é”™è¯¯ï¼šäº‹å®ä¸å­˜åœ¨\n";
            return;
        }
      
        Relationship rel;
        rel.fact_a_id = fact_a_id;
        rel.fact_b_id = fact_b_id;
        rel.relation_type = relation_type;
        rel.strength = strength;
      
        relationships.push_back(rel);
      
        cout << "[çŸ¥è¯†å›¾è°±] å…³ç³»å·²å»ºç«‹: " << relation_type 
             << " (å¼ºåº¦: " << strength << ")\n";
    }
  
    void VerifyFact(string fact_id) {
        if (knowledge_graph.find(fact_id) == 
            knowledge_graph.end()) {
            return;
        }
      
        Fact& fact = knowledge_graph[fact_id];
        fact.verification_count++;
      
        // å½“éªŒè¯æ¬¡æ•°è¶³å¤Ÿæ—¶ï¼Œæé«˜ç½®ä¿¡åº¦
        if (fact.verification_count >= 3) {
            fact.is_verified = true;
            fact.confidence = min(fact.confidence * 1.1, 1.0);
        }
      
        cout << "[çŸ¥è¯†å›¾è°±] äº‹å®éªŒè¯æ¬¡æ•°: " 
             << fact.verification_count << "\n";
    }
  
    void PrintGraph() {
        cout << "\nã€çŸ¥è¯†å›¾è°±ç»Ÿè®¡ã€‘\n";
        cout << "æ€»äº‹å®æ•°: " << knowledge_graph.size() << "\n";
        cout << "å·²éªŒè¯äº‹å®: ";
      
        int verified_count = 0;
        for (auto& [id, fact] : knowledge_graph) {
            if (fact.is_verified) verified_count++;
        }
        cout << verified_count << "\n";
      
        cout << "å…³ç³»æ•°: " << relationships.size() << "\n";
      
        cout << "\nã€äº‹å®è¯¦æƒ…ã€‘\n";
        for (auto& [id, fact] : knowledge_graph) {
            cout << "  " << id << ": ";
            cout << fact.content.substr(0, 60) << "...\n";
            cout << "    ç½®ä¿¡åº¦: " << fact.confidence;
            cout << " | éªŒè¯: " << fact.verification_count << "æ¬¡";
            cout << " | æ¥æº: " << fact.sources.size() << "\n";
        }
    }
  
    double GetOverallKnowledgeQuality() {
        if (knowledge_graph.empty()) return 0.0;
      
        double total = 0;
        for (auto& [id, fact] : knowledge_graph) {
            total += fact.confidence;
        }
        return total / knowledge_graph.size();
    }
};

// ============ å¢å¼ºçš„AIæ¨ç†å¼•æ“ ============
class AdvancedAIReasoning {
private:
    int generation;
    double learning_rate;
    KnowledgeRepresentation* knowledge;
  
public:
    struct ResearchResult {
        string hypothesis;
        vector<string> supporting_facts;
        vector<string> contradicting_facts;
        double overall_confidence;
        vector<string> next_questions;
        int generation;
    };
  
    AdvancedAIReasoning(KnowledgeRepresentation* kb)
        : generation(0), learning_rate(0.01), knowledge(kb) {}
  
    // æ·±åº¦æ¨ç†ï¼šç”Ÿæˆå‡è®¾å’Œé—®é¢˜
    ResearchResult PerformDeepReasoning(
        string research_question,
        int depth = 3  // æ¨ç†æ·±åº¦
    ) {
        cout << "\n[AIæ¨ç†] å¼€å§‹æ·±åº¦æ¨ç†\n";
        cout << "[AIæ¨ç†] é—®é¢˜: " << research_question << "\n";
        cout << "[AIæ¨ç†] æ¨ç†æ·±åº¦: " << depth << "\n";
      
        ResearchResult result;
      
        // Step 1: ç”Ÿæˆåˆå§‹å‡è®¾
        result.hypothesis = GenerateHypothesis(
            research_question
        );
        cout << "\n[AIæ¨ç†] Step1: ç”Ÿæˆå‡è®¾\n";
        cout << "[AIæ¨ç†] å‡è®¾: " << result.hypothesis << "\n";
      
        // Step 2: é€’å½’æœç´¢æ”¯æŒè¯æ®
        cout << "\n[AIæ¨ç†] Step2: æœç´¢æ”¯æŒè¯æ®\n";
        result.supporting_facts = FindSupportingEvidence(
            result.hypothesis,
            depth
        );
      
        // Step 3: æœç´¢åé©³è¯æ®
        cout << "\n[AIæ¨ç†] Step3: æœç´¢åé©³è¯æ®\n";
        result.contradicting_facts = FindContradictions(
            result.hypothesis,
            depth
        );
      
        // Step 4: è®¡ç®—ç½®ä¿¡åº¦
        cout << "\n[AIæ¨ç†] Step4: è®¡ç®—ç½®ä¿¡åº¦\n";
        result.overall_confidence = CalculateConfidence(
            result.supporting_facts,
            result.contradicting_facts
        );
      
        cout << "[AIæ¨ç†] ç½®ä¿¡åº¦: " 
             << result.overall_confidence << "\n";
      
        // Step 5: ç”Ÿæˆåç»­é—®é¢˜
        cout << "\n[AIæ¨ç†] Step5: ç”Ÿæˆåç»­é—®é¢˜\n";
        result.next_questions = GenerateFollowUpQuestions(
            research_question,
            result.hypothesis
        );
      
        for (auto& q : result.next_questions) {
            cout << "[AIæ¨ç†] â†’ " << q << "\n";
        }
      
        result.generation = generation;
        generation++;
      
        return result;
    }
  
private:
    string GenerateHypothesis(string question) {
        // æ¨¡æ‹Ÿå‡è®¾ç”Ÿæˆ
        if (question.find("å¤§ç»Ÿä¸€") != string::npos) {
            return "åŸºäºå¯¹ç§°æ€§ç ´ç¼ºçš„ç”µå¼±ç»Ÿä¸€æ¨¡å‹å¯ä»¥æ‰©å±•åˆ°å¼ºæ ¸åŠ›ï¼Œ"
                   "é€šè¿‡å¼•å…¥é¢å¤–çš„è§„èŒƒåœºå’Œè´¹ç±³å­";
        } else if (question.find("æ„è¯†") != string::npos) {
            return "æ„è¯†å¯èƒ½æ˜¯ç”±é‡å­çº ç¼ åœ¨ç¥ç»å¾®ç®¡ä¸­äº§ç”Ÿçš„"
                   "å®è§‚é‡å­æ€";
        } else {
            return "å­˜åœ¨æ½œåœ¨çš„æ•°å­¦ç»“æ„ç»Ÿä¸€ä¸Šè¿°ç°è±¡";
        }
    }
  
    vector<string> FindSupportingEvidence(
        string hypothesis,
        int depth
    ) {
        vector<string> evidence;
        evidence.push_back("è¯æ®1: å®éªŒæ•°æ®Aæ”¯æŒè¯¥å‡è®¾");
        evidence.push_back("è¯æ®2: ç†è®ºæ¨å¯¼Bä¸è¯¥å‡è®¾ä¸€è‡´");
        evidence.push_back("è¯æ®3: å·²çŸ¥ç»“æœCå¯ç”±è¯¥å‡è®¾æ¨å¯¼");
        return evidence;
    }
  
    vector<string> FindContradictions(
        string hypothesis,
        int depth
    ) {
        vector<string> contradictions;
        // æœ‰20%çš„æ¦‚ç‡æ‰¾åˆ°åé©³
        if (rand() % 5 == 0) {
            contradictions.push_back("åé©³1: å®éªŒCä¸è¯¥å‡è®¾çŸ›ç›¾");
        }
        return contradictions;
    }
  
    double CalculateConfidence(
        vector<string>& supporting,
        vector<string>& contradicting
    ) {
        if (supporting.empty()) return 0.1;
      
        double confidence = (double)supporting.size() / 
                          (supporting.size() + 
                           contradicting.size() + 1);
        return min(confidence, 0.95);
    }
  
    vector<string> GenerateFollowUpQuestions(
        string original_q,
        string hypothesis
    ) {
        vector<string> questions;
        questions.push_back("å¦‚ä½•å®éªŒéªŒè¯è¯¥å‡è®¾ï¼Ÿ");
        questions.push_back("è¯¥å‡è®¾ä¸æ—¢æœ‰ç†è®ºæœ‰ä»€ä¹ˆå…³ç³»ï¼Ÿ");
        questions.push_back("æ˜¯å¦å­˜åœ¨åä¾‹æˆ–ç‰¹æ®Šæƒ…å†µï¼Ÿ");
        questions.push_back("è¯¥å‡è®¾çš„æ•°å­¦å®Œå¤‡æ€§å¦‚ä½•ï¼Ÿ");
        return questions;
    }
};

// ============ ç¤¾åŒºéªŒè¯ç³»ç»Ÿ ============
class CommunityVerification {
public:
    struct Reviewer {
        string id;
        string name;
        string expertise;  // ä¸“ä¸šé¢†åŸŸ
        int reviews_done;
        double accuracy_rate;  // å†å²å‡†ç¡®ç‡
        double reputation;
    };
  
    struct Review {
        string review_id;
        string fact_id;
        string reviewer_id;
        bool verdict;  // true=æ”¯æŒ, false=åå¯¹
        string reasoning;
        double confidence;
        long timestamp;
    };
  
private:
    map<string, Reviewer> reviewers;
    vector<Review> reviews;
  
public:
    void RegisterReviewer(
        string id,
        string name,
        string expertise
    ) {
        Reviewer reviewer;
        reviewer.id = id;
        reviewer.name = name;
        reviewer.expertise = expertise;
        reviewer.reviews_done = 0;
        reviewer.accuracy_rate = 0.5;
        reviewer.reputation = 1.0;
      
        reviewers[id] = reviewer;
        cout << "[ç¤¾åŒº] æ³¨å†Œè¯„å®¡å‘˜: " << name 
             << " (ä¸“ä¸š: " << expertise << ")\n";
    }
  
    void SubmitReview(
        string fact_id,
        string reviewer_id,
        bool verdict,
        string reasoning,
        double confidence
    ) {
        if (reviewers.find(reviewer_id) == 
            reviewers.end()) {
            cout << "[ç¤¾åŒº] è¯„å®¡å‘˜ä¸å­˜åœ¨\n";
            return;
        }
      
        Review review;
        review.review_id = "REV_" + to_string(
            chrono::high_resolution_clock::
            now().time_since_epoch().count()
        );
        review.fact_id = fact_id;
        review.reviewer_id = reviewer_id;
        review.verdict = verdict;
        review.reasoning = reasoning;
        review.confidence = confidence;
        review.timestamp = GetCurrentTime();
      
        reviews.push_back(review);
      
        Reviewer& reviewer = reviewers[reviewer_id];
        reviewer.reviews_done++;
      
        cout << "[ç¤¾åŒº] è¯„å®¡å®Œæˆ: " << reviewers[reviewer_id].name
             << " (" << (verdict ? "æ”¯æŒ" : "åå¯¹") << ")\n";
    }
  
    double GetCommunityConsensus(string fact_id) {
        vector<Review> fact_reviews;
        for (auto& rev : reviews) {
            if (rev.fact_id == fact_id) {
                fact_reviews.push_back(rev);
            }
        }
      
        if (fact_reviews.empty()) return 0.5;
      
        double total_confidence = 0;
        int support_count = 0;
      
        for (auto& rev : fact_reviews) {
            if (rev.verdict) {
                support_count++;
                total_confidence += rev.confidence;
            } else {
                total_confidence -= rev.confidence;
            }
        }
      
        return (support_count + total_confidence) / 
               (2.0 * fact_reviews.size());
    }
  
    void PrintCommunityStats() {
        cout << "\nã€ç¤¾åŒºç»Ÿè®¡ã€‘\n";
        cout << "æ³¨å†Œè¯„å®¡å‘˜: " << reviewers.size() << "\n";
        cout << "å®Œæˆè¯„å®¡: " << reviews.size() << "\n";
      
        cout << "\nã€è¯„å®¡å‘˜å£°èª‰æ’åã€‘\n";
        vector<pair<string, double>> rep_ranking;
        for (auto& [id, reviewer] : reviewers) {
            rep_ranking.push_back({reviewer.name, 
                                   reviewer.reputation});
        }
        sort(rep_ranking.begin(), rep_ranking.end(),
             [](auto& a, auto& b) {
                 return a.second > b.second;
             });
      
        for (int i = 0; i < min(5, (int)rep_ranking.size()); i++) {
            cout << "  #" << (i+1) << " " << rep_ranking[i].first
                 << ": " << rep_ranking[i].second << " â­\n";
        }
    }
};

// ============ åŒºå—é“¾è®°å½•ç³»ç»Ÿ ============
class BlockchainRecorder {
private:
    vector<string> transaction_log;
    map<string, string> merkle_tree;
  
public:
    struct InferenceTransaction {
        string tx_id;
        string ai_model_hash;
        string research_question;
        string hypothesis;
        vector<string> facts_generated;
        double confidence;
        string zkproof;
        long timestamp;
        string block_hash;
    };
  
    vector<InferenceTransaction> transactions;
  
    void RecordInference(
        string model_hash,
        string question,
        string hypothesis,
        vector<string> facts,
        double confidence
    ) {
        InferenceTransaction tx;
        tx.tx_id = "TX_" + to_string(
            chrono::high_resolution_clock::
            now().time_since_epoch().count()
        );
        tx.ai_model_hash = model_hash;
        tx.research_question = question;
        tx.hypothesis = hypothesis;
        tx.facts_generated = facts;
        tx.confidence = confidence;
        tx.zkproof = GenerateZKProof(hypothesis);
        tx.timestamp = GetCurrentTime();
        tx.block_hash = ComputeBlockHash(tx);
      
        transactions.push_back(tx);
      
        cout << "\n[åŒºå—é“¾] äº¤æ˜“å·²è®°å½•\n";
        cout << "[åŒºå—é“¾] äº¤æ˜“ID: " << tx.tx_id << "\n";
        cout << "[åŒºå—é“¾] å—å“ˆå¸Œ: " << tx.block_hash 
             << "\n";
    }
  
    void PrintBlockchainStats() {
        cout << "\nã€åŒºå—é“¾ç»Ÿè®¡ã€‘\n";
        cout << "æ€»äº¤æ˜“æ•°: " << transactions.size() << "\n";
      
        int total_facts = 0;
        double avg_confidence = 0;
      
        for (auto& tx : transactions) {
            total_facts += tx.facts_generated.size();
            avg_confidence += tx.confidence;
        }
      
        cout << "ç”Ÿæˆæ€»äº‹å®æ•°: " << total_facts << "\n";
        cout << "å¹³å‡ç½®ä¿¡åº¦: " 
             << (avg_confidence / transactions.size()) << "\n";
    }
  
private:
    string GenerateZKProof(string hypothesis) {
        return "ZK_" + to_string(
            hash<string>{}(hypothesis)
        );
    }
  
    string ComputeBlockHash(InferenceTransaction& tx) {
        string data = tx.tx_id + tx.hypothesis + 
                     to_string(tx.timestamp);
        return "BLOCK_" + to_string(
            hash<string>{}(data)
        );
    }
};

// ============ ä¸»ç³»ç»Ÿåè°ƒå™¨ ============
class AIResearchSystem {
private:
    AIModel* ai_model;
    KnowledgeRepresentation knowledge_graph;
    AdvancedAIReasoning reasoning_engine;
    CommunityVerification community;
    BlockchainRecorder blockchain;
  
    int epoch = 0;
    vector<string> research_agenda = {
        "å¤§ç»Ÿä¸€å®šç†çš„æ•°å­¦åŸºç¡€æ˜¯ä»€ä¹ˆï¼Ÿ",
        "é‡å­å¼•åŠ›ä¸å¹¿ä¹‰ç›¸å¯¹è®ºå¦‚ä½•ç»Ÿä¸€ï¼Ÿ",
        "æ„è¯†çš„ç‰©ç†åŸºç¡€æ˜¯ä»€ä¹ˆï¼Ÿ",
        "æ˜¯å¦å­˜åœ¨è¶…è¶Šç°æœ‰æ•°å­¦æ¡†æ¶çš„æ›´æ·±å±‚ç»“æ„ï¼Ÿ",
        "å®‡å®™çš„åˆå§‹æ¡ä»¶å¦‚ä½•ç”±ç‰©ç†å®šå¾‹å†³å®šï¼Ÿ"
    };
  
public:
    AIResearchSystem(AIModel* model)
        : ai_model(model), reasoning_engine(&knowledge_graph) {}
  
    void Initialize() {
        cout << "========== AIç ”ç©¶ç³»ç»Ÿåˆå§‹åŒ– ==========\n\n";
      
        // åˆå§‹åŒ–ç¤¾åŒºè¯„å®¡å‘˜
        cout << "ã€åˆå§‹åŒ–ç¤¾åŒºè¯„å®¡å‘˜ã€‘\n";
        community.RegisterReviewer(
            "REV001", "Dr. Alice", "ç†è®ºç‰©ç†"
        );
        community.RegisterReviewer(
            "REV002", "Dr. Bob", "æ•°å­¦"
        );
        community.RegisterReviewer(
            "REV003", "Dr. Charlie", "è®¡ç®—æœºç§‘å­¦"
        );
        community.RegisterReviewer(
            "REV004", "Dr. Diana", "å“²å­¦"
        );
      
        cout << "\n[ç³»ç»Ÿ] åˆå§‹åŒ–å®Œæˆ\n";
    }
  
    void RunResearchEpoch() {
        epoch++;
        cout << "\n\n"
             << "â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”\n"
             << "ç ”ç©¶è½®æ¬¡ #" << epoch << "\n"
             << "â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”\n";
      
        // é€‰æ‹©ç ”ç©¶é—®é¢˜
        string research_q = research_agenda[
            (epoch - 1) % research_agenda.size()
        ];
      
        cout << "\nã€å½“å‰ç ”ç©¶é—®é¢˜ã€‘\n" << research_q << "\n";
      
        // AIè¿›è¡Œæ·±åº¦æ¨ç†
        cout << "\nã€AIæ¨ç†è¿‡ç¨‹ã€‘\n";
        auto result = reasoning_engine.PerformDeepReasoning(
            research_q,
            epoch  // æ¨ç†æ·±åº¦éšè½®æ¬¡å¢åŠ 
        );
      
        // è®°å½•ç”Ÿæˆçš„äº‹å®
        cout << "\nã€äº‹å®è®°å½•ã€‘\n";
        vector<string> fact_ids;
        for (auto& evidence : result.supporting_facts) {
            string fact_id = knowledge_graph.AddFact(
                evidence,
                result.overall_confidence,
                {"epoch_" + to_string(epoch)}
            );
            fact_ids.push_back(fact_id);
        }
      
        // ç¤¾åŒºå®¡æŸ¥
        cout << "\nã€ç¤¾åŒºå®¡æŸ¥è¿‡ç¨‹ã€‘\n";
        ReviewFactsInCommunity(fact_ids);
      
        // å»ºç«‹äº‹å®ä¹‹é—´çš„å…³ç³»
        cout << "\nã€çŸ¥è¯†å…³ç³»å»ºç«‹ã€‘\n";
        if (fact_ids.size() >= 2) {
            knowledge_graph.AddRelationship(
                fact_ids[0],
                fact_ids[1],
                "supports",
                0.8
            );
        }
      
        // ä¸Šé“¾è®°å½•
        cout << "\nã€ä¸Šé“¾è®°å½•ã€‘\n";
        blockchain.RecordInference(
            ai_model->GetModelHash(),
            research_q,
            result.hypothesis,
            fact_ids,
            result.overall_confidence
        );
      
        // æ¨¡å‹è‡ªè¿­ä»£
        cout << "\nã€æ¨¡å‹è‡ªè¿­ä»£ã€‘\n";
        ImproveModel();
    }
  
    void ReviewFactsInCommunity(vector<string> fact_ids) {
        vector<string> reviewer_ids = {
            "REV001", "REV002", "REV003"
        };
      
        for (auto& fact_id : fact_ids) {
            // æ¯ä¸ªäº‹å®è¢«å¤šä¸ªè¯„å®¡å‘˜å®¡æŸ¥
            for (auto& rev_id : reviewer_ids) {
                bool verdict = (rand() % 10) > 2;  // 70%æ¦‚ç‡æ”¯æŒ
              
                community.SubmitReview(
                    fact_id,
                    rev_id,
                    verdict,
                    "åŸºäºæˆ‘çš„ä¸“ä¸šçŸ¥è¯†è¿›è¡Œè¯„å®¡",
                    0.7 + (rand() % 30) / 100.0
                );
              
                // å¦‚æœé€šè¿‡ç¤¾åŒºå…±è¯†ï¼Œæ›´æ–°çŸ¥è¯†åº“
                if (community.GetCommunityConsensus(fact_id) > 0.6) {
                    knowledge_graph.VerifyFact(fact_id);
                }
            }
        }
    }
  
    void ImproveModel() {
        cout << "[ç³»ç»Ÿ] åŸºäºæ­¤è½®å‘ç°è¿›è¡Œæ¨¡å‹æ”¹è¿›\n";
      
        // åœ¨çœŸå®ç³»ç»Ÿä¸­ï¼Œè¿™é‡Œä¼šï¼š
        // 1. å¾®è°ƒæ¨¡å‹å‚æ•°
        // 2. æ›´æ–°åµŒå…¥å‘é‡
        // 3. ä¼˜åŒ–æ¨ç†ç­–ç•¥
      
        cout << "[ç³»ç»Ÿ] æ¨¡å‹ç‰ˆæœ¬æ›´æ–°\n";
        // ai_model->FineTune(knowledge_graph.GetAllFacts());
    }
  
    void PrintFullReport() {
        cout << "\n\n"
             << "========== å®Œæ•´ç³»ç»ŸæŠ¥å‘Š ==========\n";
      
        cout << "\nã€ç ”ç©¶è¿›å±•ç»Ÿè®¡ã€‘\n";
        cout << "å®Œæˆè½®æ¬¡: " << epoch << "\n";
        cout << "çŸ¥è¯†åº“è´¨é‡: " 
             << (knowledge_graph.GetOverallKnowledgeQuality() * 100)
             << "%\n";
      
        knowledge_graph.PrintGraph();
        community.PrintCommunityStats();
        blockchain.PrintBlockchainStats();
      
        cout << "\nã€ç³»ç»Ÿä¼˜åŠ¿æ€»ç»“ã€‘\n";
        cout << "âœ“ AIåœ¨é“¾ä¸‹é«˜æ•ˆè¿è¡Œ\n";
        cout << "âœ“ æ¨ç†è¿‡ç¨‹é€šè¿‡ZKè¯æ˜åœ¨é“¾ä¸ŠéªŒè¯\n";
        cout << "âœ“ çŸ¥è¯†ç”±åˆ†å¸ƒå¼ç¤¾åŒºéªŒè¯\n";
        cout << "âœ“ æ‰€æœ‰å‘ç°ä¸å¯ç¯¡æ”¹åœ°è®°å½•\n";
        cout << "âœ“ æ¿€åŠ±æœºåˆ¶é¼“åŠ±å‚ä¸\n";
        cout << "âœ“ é€æ˜çš„ã€å¯å®¡è®¡çš„ç ”ç©¶è¿‡ç¨‹\n";
    }
};

// ============ ä¸»ç¨‹åº ============
int main() {

    vector<ResearchResult> competing_hypotheses;

    vector<ResearchResult> ParallelInference(

        cout << "\n[AI-Innovative] æ¨ç†ä¸­...\n";

    void DebateResults(

### **å…·ä½“æŠ€æœ¯æ ˆé€‰æ‹©**

```cpp
// ==========================================
// ã€ç¬¬äºŒæ­¥ã€‘é€‰æ‹©æŠ€æœ¯æ ˆ
// ==========================================

ã€AIæ¨¡å‹å±‚ã€‘
â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”

é€‰é¡¹A: å¼€æºåŸºç¡€æ¨¡å‹å¾®è°ƒï¼ˆæ¨èåˆæœŸï¼‰
  - åŸºç¡€æ¨¡å‹ï¼šLLaMA 2 70B æˆ– Mistral Large
  - ä¸ºä»€ä¹ˆï¼šå¼€æºã€å¯æ§ã€å¯åœ¨æœ¬åœ°è¿è¡Œ
  - å¾®è°ƒæ–¹å¼ï¼šLoRAï¼ˆä½ç§©é€‚é…ï¼‰
  - æˆæœ¬ï¼šä¸€å¼ A100 GPUå¯å¤„ç†
  - ä¼˜ç‚¹ï¼šå¿«é€Ÿè¿­ä»£ã€æˆæœ¬ä½
  - ç¼ºç‚¹ï¼šèƒ½åŠ›æœ‰é™

  ä»£ç æ¡†æ¶ï¼š
  ```
  HuggingFace Transformers + PEFT (LoRA)
  â”œâ”€ åŠ è½½LLaMA 2 70B
  â”œâ”€ å†»ç»“ä¸»è¦å‚æ•°
  â”œâ”€ ä»…å¾®è°ƒLoRAæ¨¡å—
  â”œâ”€ åœ¨ç§‘å­¦è®ºæ–‡æ•°æ®é›†ä¸Šè®­ç»ƒ
  â””â”€ è¾“å‡ºï¼šç§‘å­¦æ¨ç†èƒ½åŠ›å¢å¼ºçš„æ¨¡å‹
  ```

é€‰é¡¹B: è‡ªå»ºå°è§„æ¨¡åŸºç¡€æ¨¡å‹ï¼ˆä¸­æœŸï¼‰
  - å‚æ•°è§„æ¨¡ï¼š7B - 13B
  - ä¸ºä»€ä¹ˆï¼šå®Œå…¨å¯æ§
  - è®­ç»ƒæ•°æ®ï¼šç§‘å­¦è®ºæ–‡ + æ•™ç§‘ä¹¦ + æ¨ç†è¿‡ç¨‹
  - æˆæœ¬ï¼š8å°A100 GPUï¼Œè®­ç»ƒ1ä¸ªæœˆ
  - ä¼˜ç‚¹ï¼šå®Œå…¨å®šåˆ¶åŒ–
  - ç¼ºç‚¹ï¼šéœ€è¦ä¸“ä¸šå›¢é˜Ÿ

é€‰é¡¹C: ä¸“æœ‰æ¨¡å‹API + è‡ªç ”æ¨ç†å±‚ï¼ˆé«˜çº§ï¼‰
  - ä½¿ç”¨ï¼šOpenAI GPT-4 / Anthropic Claude
  - ä¸ºä»€ä¹ˆï¼šèƒ½åŠ›æœ€å¼º
  - è‡ªç ”ï¼šåœ¨å…¶ä¸Šæ„å»ºç§‘å­¦æ¨ç†æ¡†æ¶
  - æˆæœ¬ï¼šAPIè°ƒç”¨è´¹ç”¨
  - ä¼˜ç‚¹ï¼šæ— éœ€è®­ç»ƒï¼Œç›´æ¥ç”¨æœ€å¼ºæ¨¡å‹
  - ç¼ºç‚¹ï¼šæˆæœ¬é«˜ã€ä¸å¯æ§ã€ä¾èµ–ç¬¬ä¸‰æ–¹

æ¨èè·¯çº¿ï¼š
  Year 1: é€‰é¡¹Aï¼ˆå¿«é€ŸéªŒè¯ï¼‰
  Year 2: è¿‡æ¸¡åˆ°é€‰é¡¹Bï¼ˆè‡ªä¸»æ€§ï¼‰
  Year 3+: æ··åˆï¼ˆB + ä¼˜é€‰çš„Cï¼‰


ã€æ¨ç†æ¡†æ¶ã€‘
â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”

ä¸ºäº†è®©AIåš"ç§‘å­¦æ¨ç†"è€Œé"èŠå¤©"ï¼š

```python
# ä¼ªä»£ç ï¼šç§‘å­¦æ¨ç†æ¡†æ¶

class ScientificReasoningEngine:
    def __init__(self, base_model):
        self.model = base_model
        self.knowledge_graph = KnowledgeGraph()
        self.formal_verifier = FormalVerifier()  # éªŒè¯é€»è¾‘
      
    def reason_on_research_question(self, question):
        """
        å¤šæ­¥éª¤æ¨ç†
        """
      
        # Step 1: é—®é¢˜åˆ†è§£
        subquestions = self.decompose(question)
      
        # Step 2: èƒŒæ™¯çŸ¥è¯†æ£€ç´¢
        relevant_facts = self.knowledge_graph.retrieve(
            question, 
            top_k=50
        )
      
        # Step 3: å¤šè·¯å¾„æ¨ç†ï¼ˆå…³é”®ï¼ï¼‰
        reasoning_paths = []
      
        for _ in range(3):  # å°è¯•3æ¡ä¸åŒè·¯å¾„
            path = self.generate_reasoning_path(
                subquestions,
                relevant_facts
            )
            reasoning_paths.append(path)
      
        # Step 4: å½¢å¼åŒ–éªŒè¯
        verified_paths = []
        for path in reasoning_paths:
            if self.formal_verifier.verify(path):
                verified_paths.append(path)
      
        # Step 5: ç”Ÿæˆå‡è®¾
        hypotheses = []
        for path in verified_paths:
            hypo = self.synthesize_hypothesis(path)
            hypotheses.append(hypo)
      
        # Step 6: è¯„ä¼°å’Œæ’åº
        ranked_hypotheses = self.rank_by_novelty(
            hypotheses
        )
      
        return {
            'hypotheses': ranked_hypotheses,
            'reasoning_paths': verified_paths,
            'confidence': self.compute_confidence(
                ranked_hypotheses
            )
        }
  
    def generate_reasoning_path(self, subquestions, facts):
        """
        é“¾å¼æ€ç»´æç¤ºï¼ˆChain of Thoughtï¼‰
        ä½†æ›´åŠ ç»“æ„åŒ–
        """
        prompt = self._construct_prompt(
            subquestions,
            facts
        )
      
        response = self.model.generate(
            prompt,
            temperature=0.7,  # æœ‰åˆ›æ„ä½†ä¸å¤ªéšæ„
            max_tokens=2000,
            num_beams=5  # beam searchæ‰¾åˆ°æœ€ä½³è·¯å¾„
        )
      
        # è§£ææ¨¡å‹è¾“å‡ºä¸ºç»“æ„åŒ–æ¨ç†è·¯å¾„
        path = self._parse_reasoning_steps(response)
        return path
```

æ¨èä½¿ç”¨çš„æ¡†æ¶åº“ï¼š

  âœ“ LlamaIndexï¼ˆçŸ¥è¯†åº“æ£€ç´¢å¢å¼ºï¼‰

  âœ“ Solidityï¼ˆæœ€æˆç†Ÿï¼‰
  âœ“ Vyperï¼ˆæ›¿ä»£æ–¹æ¡ˆï¼‰

å…³é”®åˆçº¦ï¼š

```solidity
pragma solidity ^0.8.0;

// 1. æ¨ç†è®°å½•åˆçº¦
contract InferenceRegistry {
    struct Inference {
        bytes32 id;
        address ai_operator;
        bytes32 hypothesis_hash;
        uint256 confidence;      // 0-10000 (0-100%)
        bytes32 zk_proof;        // ZKè¯æ˜
        uint256 timestamp;
        bool verified;
    }
  
    mapping(bytes32 => Inference) inferences;
  
    function recordInference(
        bytes32 hypothesis_hash,
        uint256 confidence,
        bytes32 zk_proof
    ) external {
        Inference memory inf = Inference({
            id: keccak256(abi.encodePacked(
                msg.sender,
                block.timestamp
            )),
            ai_operator: msg.sender,
            hypothesis_hash: hypothesis_hash,
            confidence: confidence,
            zk_proof: zk_proof,
            timestamp: block.timestamp,
            verified: false
        });
      
        inferences[inf.id] = inf;
        emit InferenceRecorded(inf.id);
    }
}

// 2. ç¤¾åŒºéªŒè¯åˆçº¦
contract CommunityVerification {
    struct Review {
        bytes32 inference_id;
        address reviewer;
        bool verdict;  // true = support, false = oppose
        uint256 confidence;
        string reasoning;
    }
  
    mapping(bytes32 => Review[]) reviews;
    mapping(address => uint256) reviewer_reputation;
  
    function submitReview(
        bytes32 inference_id,
        bool verdict,
        uint256 confidence,
        string calldata reasoning
    ) external {
        Review memory review = Review({
            inference_id: inference_id,
            reviewer: msg.sender,
            verdict: verdict,
            confidence: confidence,
            reasoning: reasoning
        });
      
        reviews[inference_id].push(review);
      
        // æ›´æ–°å£°èª‰ï¼ˆåŸºäºæŠ•ç¥¨æƒé‡ï¼‰
        if (verdict) {
            reviewer_reputation[msg.sender] += confidence;
        }
    }
  
    function getCommunityConsensus(
        bytes32 inference_id
    ) external view returns (uint256) {
        Review[] storage rev = reviews[inference_id];
      
        uint256 support = 0;
        uint256 oppose = 0;
      
        for (uint i = 0; i < rev.length; i++) {
            if (rev[i].verdict) {
                support += rev[i].confidence;
            } else {
                oppose += rev[i].confidence;
            }
        }
      
        if (support + oppose == 0) return 50;
        return (support * 100) / (support + oppose);
    }
}

// 3. æ¿€åŠ±åˆçº¦
contract ResearchIncentives {
    IERC20 public reward_token;
  
    uint256 public reward_per_inference = 1e18;  // 1 token
    uint256 public reward_per_review = 0.1e18;    // 0.1 token
    uint256 public reward_bonus_if_verified = 2e18;  // é¢å¤–å¥–åŠ±
  
    function claimInferenceReward(
        bytes32 inference_id
    ) external {
        InferenceRegistry registry = InferenceRegistry(...);
        Inference memory inf = registry.getInference(
            inference_id
        );
      
        require(inf.ai_operator == msg.sender);
      
        uint256 reward = reward_per_inference;
      
        // å¦‚æœæ¨ç†å¾—åˆ°äº†ç¤¾åŒºéªŒè¯
        uint256 consensus = 
            CommunityVerification(...).getCommunityConsensus(
            inference_id
        );
      
        if (consensus > 60) {
            reward += reward_bonus_if_verified;
        }
      
        reward_token.transfer(msg.sender, reward);
    }
}
```

## åå…­ã€é£é™©åº”å¯¹æ–¹æ¡ˆ

  âœ“ ä¸‰å±‚è´¨é‡é—¨æ§›
    1) AIå†…éƒ¨éªŒè¯ï¼ˆå½¢å¼åŒ–æ£€æŸ¥ï¼‰

   â†’ äººç±»æ€ç»´èƒ½åŠ› +?å€

ã€è¿™ä¸ªç³»ç»Ÿçš„ç‹¬ç‰¹æ€§ã€‘
â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”

ä¸å…¶ä»–å·¥å…·ä¸åŒï¼š
  âœ— æœ›è¿œé•œæ˜¯è¢«åŠ¨çš„ï¼ˆåªæ˜¯æ”¾å¤§ï¼‰
  âœ“ è¿™ä¸ªç³»ç»Ÿæ˜¯ä¸»åŠ¨çš„ï¼ˆä¼šè‡ªå·±æ€è€ƒï¼‰

  âœ— è®¡ç®—æœºæ˜¯å¬å‘½çš„ï¼ˆæŒ‰ç…§ç¨‹åºï¼‰

  âœ“ è¿™ä¸ªç³»ç»Ÿæ‰©å±•æ€ç»´ï¼ˆå¤§è„‘ï¼‰

è¿™æ˜¯äººç±»å†å²ä¸Šç¬¬ä¸€æ¬¡ï¼š
  ğŸ¯ äººç±»åˆ›é€ äº†ä¸€ä¸ª"æ™ºèƒ½ä½“"æ¥å¸®åŠ©è‡ªå·±æ€è€ƒ

åæœï¼š
  æ­£é¢ï¼šåŠ é€Ÿäººç±»æ–‡æ˜å‘å±•

  "ç§‘å­¦æ˜¯é€šè¿‡å¤šä¸ªæ™ºèƒ½ä½“ï¼ˆäººç±»å’ŒAIï¼‰
   çš„äº’åŠ¨è¿‡ç¨‹ï¼Œå…±åŒé€¼è¿‘çœŸç†"

  âœ“ çœŸç†çš„å®šä¹‰ä»"è¢«å‘ç°"åˆ°"è¢«å»ºæ„"

  âœ“ ç§‘å­¦å˜å¾—æ°‘ä¸»åŒ–

æœ€æ·±å±‚çš„é—®é¢˜ï¼š
  "å¦‚æœAIèƒ½å’Œäººç±»ä¸€æ ·æ€è€ƒï¼Œ
   é‚£ä¹ˆæ€è€ƒçš„æœ¬è´¨æ˜¯ä»€ä¹ˆï¼Ÿ
 
   å¦‚æœè¿™ä¸ªç³»ç»Ÿæœ€ç»ˆæ¯”æ‰€æœ‰äººç±»ç§‘å­¦å®¶éƒ½èªæ˜ï¼Œ
   äººç±»çš„è§’è‰²æ˜¯ä»€ä¹ˆï¼Ÿ"

æˆ‘çš„è§‚ç‚¹ï¼š

        cout << "  å¼•ç”¨ï¼šå·²è¢«100+è®ºæ–‡å¼•ç”¨\n";
      
        breakthrough_count++;
        SimulateResearchCycle("é‡å­è›‹ç™½è´¨æ•ˆåº”", 0.85);

        cout << "  é¢˜ç›®ï¼šæ–°çš„ææ–™è®¾è®¡åŸç†\n";

        cout << "  ğŸ“Š å­¦æœ¯è®ºæ–‡ï¼š50+\n";
        cout << "  ğŸ“Š çŸ¥è¯†äº‹å®ï¼š50000+\n";
        cout << "  ğŸ“Š ç¤¾åŒºå…±è¯†ï¼š78%\n";
        cout << "  ğŸ“Š çªç ´æ€§å‘ç°ï¼š2\n";
        cout << "  ğŸ“Š èèµ„æ€»é¢ï¼š$30M+\n";
    }
  
    void SimulateResearchCycle(
        string hypothesis,
        double confidence
    ) {
        total_research_cycles++;
      
        cout << "\n  â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€\n";
        cout << "  æ¨ç†å‘¨æœŸ #" << total_research_cycles << "\n";
        cout << "  â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€\n";
        cout << "  å‡è®¾ï¼š" << hypothesis << "\n";
        cout << "  ç½®ä¿¡åº¦ï¼š" << (confidence * 100) << "%\n";
      
        // æ¨¡æ‹Ÿç¤¾åŒºéªŒè¯
        int reviewers = 5 + (rand() % 10);
        int support = (int)(reviewers * confidence);
      
        cout << "  ç¤¾åŒºè¯„å®¡ï¼š" << support << "/" << reviewers 
             << " æ”¯æŒ\n";
      
        if (confidence > 0.7) {
            cout << "  çŠ¶æ€ï¼šâœ… é€šè¿‡éªŒè¯\n";
            cout << "  ä¸Šé“¾è®°å½•ï¼šå·²ä¿å­˜åˆ°åŒºå—é“¾\n";
        } else {

åç«¯ï¼ˆPython FastAPIï¼‰ï¼š
```python
# ç®€åŒ–çš„æ¨ç†ç«¯ç‚¹
@app.post("/infer")
async def infer(question: str):
    # 1. ä»çŸ¥è¯†åº“æ£€ç´¢
    facts = knowledge_db.retrieve(question)
  
    # 2. è°ƒç”¨LLaMAæ¨¡å‹
    hypothesis = llama_model.generate(
        question, facts
    )
  
    # 3. å½¢å¼åŒ–éªŒè¯
    verified = formal_checker.verify(hypothesis)
  
    # 4. å†™å…¥æ•°æ®åº“
    result = {
        "hypothesis": hypothesis,
        "confidence": verified.confidence,
        "tx_hash": blockchain.record(hypothesis)
    }
  
    return result
```

å‰ç«¯ï¼ˆNext.jsç®€åŒ–ç‰ˆï¼‰ï¼š
```javascript
// ç”¨æˆ·æäº¤é—®é¢˜çš„ç•Œé¢
export default function ResearchPage() {
  const [question, setQuestion] = useState("")
  const [results, setResults] = useState([])

  async function handleSubmit() {
    const response = await fetch("/api/infer", {
      method: "POST",
      body: JSON.stringify({ question })
    })
  
    const data = await response.json()
    setResults([...results, data])
  }

  return (
    <div>
      <textarea
        value={question}
        onChange={(e) => setQuestion(e.target.value)}
        placeholder="è¾“å…¥ç ”ç©¶é—®é¢˜..."
      />
      <button onClick={handleSubmit}>ç”Ÿæˆå‡è®¾</button>
    
      {results.map((r) => (
        <div key={r.tx_hash}>
          <p>å‡è®¾ï¼š{r.hypothesis}</p>
          <p>ç½®ä¿¡åº¦ï¼š{r.confidence}</p>
          <p>åŒºå—é“¾ï¼š{r.tx_hash}</p>
        </div>
      ))}
    </div>
  )
}
```

æ™ºèƒ½åˆçº¦ï¼ˆSolidityç®€åŒ–ç‰ˆï¼‰ï¼š
```solidity
pragma solidity ^0.8.0;

contract ResearchRegistry {
    struct Hypothesis {
        bytes32 id;
        string text;
        uint256 confidence;  // 0-100
        address submitter;
        uint256 timestamp;
    }
  
    mapping(bytes32 => Hypothesis) hypotheses;
  
    function submitHypothesis(
        string memory text,
        uint256 confidence
    ) public {
        bytes32 id = keccak256(abi.encodePacked(
            text, msg.sender, block.timestamp
        ));
      
        hypotheses[id] = Hypothesis(
            id, text, confidence, msg.sender, block.timestamp
        );
    }
}
```
